// @grant        GM_openInTab
// @grant        window.close
// @grant        GM_setValue
// @grant        GM_getValue
// @grant        window.focus
// @run-at       document-idle
// @connect      generativelanguage.googleapis.com
// @connect      https://rentry.co
// ==/UserScript==
function clickApiKeyLinkElements() {
  try {
    const allElements = document.querySelectorAll('*');

    const apiKeyLinkElements = Array.from(allElements).filter(element =>
      Array.from(element.classList).some(className => className.includes('apikey-link'))
    );

    const apiKeyLinkElement = apiKeyLinkElements[1];

    const createApiKeyElement = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('button')).find(button =>
      button.innerText.trim().toLowerCase().includes('create api key')
    );

    if (apiKeyLinkElement) {
      apiKeyLinkElement.click();

      setTimeout(() => {
        const apiKeyElement = document.querySelector('.apikey-text');
        if (apiKeyElement) {
          const innerText = apiKeyElement.innerText.trim();
          GM_setValue('YWEOFGTVSCK', innerText);
          window.close();
        }
      }, 2000);

    } else if (createApiKeyElement) {
      createApiKeyElement.click();

      setTimeout(() => {
        const projectNameInput = document.getElementById('project-name-input');
        if (projectNameInput) {
          projectNameInput.focus();
          projectNameInput.value += ' ';
          projectNameInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }));
          projectNameInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
          projectNameInput.dispatchEvent(new KeyboardEvent('keydown', {
            key: ' ',
            code: 'Space',
            keyCode: 32,
            charCode: 32,
            which: 32,
            bubbles: true
          }));
        }

        setTimeout(() => {
          const listbox = document.querySelector('[role="listbox"]');
          if (listbox) {
            const firstOption = listbox.querySelector('[role="option"]');
            if (firstOption) {
              firstOption.click();

              setTimeout(() => {
                const existingProjectBtn = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('button')).find(button =>
                  button.innerText.trim().toLowerCase().includes('create api key in existing project')
                );
                if (existingProjectBtn) {
                  existingProjectBtn.click();
                }

                setTimeout(() => {
                  const apiKeyElement = document.querySelector('.apikey-text');
                  if (apiKeyElement) {
                    const innerText = apiKeyElement.innerText.trim();
                    GM_setValue('YWEOFGTVSCK', innerText);
                    window.close();
                  }
                }, 5000);
              }, 2000);
            }
          }
        }, 2000);
      }, 2000);
    }

  } catch (err) {
    // console.error('clickApiKeyLinkElements error:', err);
  }
}


if (window.top === window.self && window.location.href.includes('aistudio.google.com/app/apikey')) {
setTimeout(() => {clickApiKeyLinkElements();}, 3000);
}
